glitch.js:3:function triggerGlitch(wrapper) {
glitch.js:4:    const img = wrapper.querySelector('#glitch-target');
glitch.js:5:    const canvas = wrapper.querySelector('#noise-canvas');
glitch.js:6:    const images = img.getAttribute('data-images').split(',');
glitch.js:8:    // 1. Sync Canvas resolution to actual rendered image size
glitch.js:9:    const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();
glitch.js:10:    canvas.width = rect.width;
glitch.js:11:    canvas.height = rect.height;
glitch.js:13:    wrapper.classList.add('glitching');
glitch.js:14:    
glitch.js:15:    let startTime = performance.now();
glitch.js:16:    const duration = 400; // Total transition time
glitch.js:18:    function animate(time) {
glitch.js:19:        let progress = (time - startTime) / duration;
glitch.js:20:        if (progress < 1) {
glitch.js:21:            drawEnderLayers(canvas, img, progress);
glitch.js:22:            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
glitch.js:23:        } else {
glitch.js:24:            canvas.getContext('2d').clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
glitch.js:25:        }
glitch.js:26:    }
glitch.js:27:    requestAnimationFrame(animate);
glitch.js:29:    // Swap source mid-way
glitch.js:30:    currentIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % images.length;
glitch.js:31:    setTimeout(() => { img.src = images[currentIndex]; }, duration / 2);
glitch.js:33:    // End effect
glitch.js:34:    setTimeout(() => { wrapper.classList.remove('glitching'); }, duration);
glitch.js:35:}
glitch.js:37:function drawEnderLayers(canvas, img, progress) {
glitch.js:38:    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
glitch.js:39:    const w = canvas.width;
glitch.js:40:    const h = canvas.height;
glitch.js:42:    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
glitch.js:43:    
glitch.js:44:    // Masking: Draw image first, then only allow painting inside it
glitch.js:45:    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h);
glitch.js:46:    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-atop';
glitch.js:48:    // Defined sensitivity layers [position, thickness, color]
glitch.js:49:    const layers = [
glitch.js:50:        { y: 0.1, th: 0.20, color: 'rgba(100, 32, 167, 0.6)' }, // Void Purple
glitch.js:51:        { y: 0.4, th: 0.10, color: 'rgba(212, 0, 255, 0.8)' }, // End Magenta
glitch.js:52:        { y: 0.7, th: 0.05, color: 'rgba(0, 255, 65, 0.7)' }   // Eye Green
glitch.js:53:    ];
glitch.js:55:    layers.forEach(layer => {
glitch.js:56:        // Move y proportionally
glitch.js:57:        const moveY = ((layer.y + progress) % 1) * h;
glitch.js:58:        const thickness = layer.th * h;
glitch.js:59:        
glitch.js:60:        const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, moveY, 0, moveY + thickness);
glitch.js:61:        grad.addColorStop(0, 'transparent');
glitch.js:62:        grad.addColorStop(0.5, layer.color);
glitch.js:63:        grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
glitch.js:65:        ctx.fillStyle = grad;
glitch.js:66:        // Padding prevents hard edges at the sweep boundaries
glitch.js:67:        ctx.fillRect(0, moveY - (h * 0.1), w, thickness + (h * 0.2));
glitch.js:68:    });
glitch.js:69:}

biomes.js:10:    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
biomes.js:11:    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
biomes.js:12:    
biomes.js:13:    // Match canvas dimensions to the image's displayed size
biomes.js:14:    canvas.width = img.clientWidth;
biomes.js:15:    canvas.height = img.clientHeight;
biomes.js:16:    
biomes.js:17:    // 2. Draw the image to the mask
biomes.js:18:    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, img.clientWidth, img.clientHeight);
biomes.js:19:    
biomes.js:20:    // 3. Get click coordinates relative to the image
biomes.js:21:    const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();
biomes.js:22:    const x = event.clientX - rect.left;
biomes.js:23:    const y = event.clientY - rect.top;
biomes.js:24:    
biomes.js:25:    // 4. Compare the pixel data at those coordinates
biomes.js:26:    // getImageData returns [R, G, B, A]. We only care about A (index 3).
biomes.js:27:    const pixelAlpha = ctx.getImageData(x, y, 1, 1).data[3];
biomes.js:28:    
biomes.js:29:    // 5. Only proceed if the clicked part is visible (Alpha > 0)
biomes.js:30:    if (pixelAlpha > 0) {
biomes.js:31:        const dataAttr = img.getAttribute('data-images');
biomes.js:32:        const images = dataAttr.split(',').map(s => s.trim());
biomes.js:33:        const currentSrc = img.getAttribute('src');
biomes.js:34:        
biomes.js:35:        // Filter out the current biome to ensure a change[span_5](start_span)[span_5](end_span)
biomes.js:36:        const availableOptions = images.filter(src => src !== currentSrc);
biomes.js:37:        const newBiome = availableOptions[Math.floor(Math.random() * availableOptions.length)];
biomes.js:38:        
biomes.js:39:        // Update the image
biomes.js:40:        img.src = newBiome;
biomes.js:41:        
biomes.js:42:        // Trigger the external glitch function[span_6](start_span)[span_6](end_span)
biomes.js:43:        if (typeof triggerGlitch === 'function') {
biomes.js:44:            triggerGlitch(wrapper);
biomes.js:45:        }
biomes.js:46:    } else {
biomes.js:47:        console.log("Click ignored: Transparent area.");
biomes.js:48:    }

clouds.js:31:        img.src = set.path;
clouds.js:33:        img.onload = () => {

clouds.js:40:            const dataUrl = bakeTexture(set);

clouds.js:46:function bakeTexture(set) {
clouds.js:47:    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
clouds.js:48:    canvas.width = set.mapW * set.blockSize;

clouds.js:53:    for (let x = 0; x < set.mapW; x++) {
clouds.js:54:        for (let y = 0; y < set.mapH; y++) {
clouds.js:55:            // fBm noise call
clouds.js:56:            const val = Noise.fBm(x * set.scale, y * (set.scale * 0.85));
clouds.js:57:            if (val > set.threshold) {
clouds.js:58:                ctx.fillRect(x * set.blockSize, y * set.blockSize, set.blockSize, set.blockSize);
clouds.js:59:            }
clouds.js:60:        }

clouds.js:83:        const moveY = -(scroll * layer.speed % layer.h);

clouds.js:97:// --- NOISE ENGINE (Fallback) ---
clouds.js:98:const Noise = new function() {
clouds.js:99:    this.p = new Uint8Array(512);
clouds.js:100:    const p256 = new Uint8Array(256).map(() => Math.random() * 256);
clouds.js:101:    for(let i=0; i<256; i++) this.p[i] = this.p[i+256] = p256[i];
clouds.js:102:    this.fade = t => t * t * t * (t * (t * 6 - 15) + 10);
clouds.js:103:    this.lerp = (t, a, b) => a + t * (b - a);
clouds.js:104:    this.grad = (hash, x, y) => {
clouds.js:105:        const h = hash & 15, u = h < 8 ? x : y, v = h < 4 ? y : h === 12 || h === 14 ? x : 0;
clouds.js:106:        return ((h & 1) === 0 ? u : -u) + ((h & 2) === 0 ? v : -v);
clouds.js:107:    };
clouds.js:108:    this.perlin = (x, y) => {
clouds.js:109:        const X = Math.floor(x) & 255, Y = Math.floor(y) & 255;
clouds.js:110:        x -= Math.floor(x); y -= Math.floor(y);
clouds.js:111:        const u = this.fade(x), v = this.fade(y);
clouds.js:112:        const A = this.p[X]+Y, AA = this.p[A], AB = this.p[A+1], B = this.p[X+1]+Y, BA = this.p[B], BB = this.p[B+1];
clouds.js:113:        return this.lerp(v, this.lerp(u, this.grad(this.p[AA], x, y), this.grad(this.p[BA], x-1, y)),
clouds.js:114:                            this.lerp(u, this.grad(this.p[AB], x, y-1), this.grad(this.p[BB], x-1, y-1)));
clouds.js:115:    };
clouds.js:116:    this.fBm = (x, y) => {
clouds.js:117:        let total = 0, amp = 1, freq = 1, max = 0;
clouds.js:118:        for(let i=0; i<4; i++) {
clouds.js:119:            total += this.perlin(x * freq, y * freq) * amp;
clouds.js:120:            max += amp; amp *= 0.5; freq *= 2;
clouds.js:121:        }
clouds.js:122:        return (total / max + 1) / 2;
clouds.js:123:    };
clouds.js:124:};
clouds.js:126:initSky();

glitch-test/glitch.js:9:    const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();
glitch-test/glitch.js:10:    canvas.width = rect.width;
glitch-test/glitch.js:11:    canvas.height = rect.height;
glitch-test/glitch.js:13:    wrapper.classList.add('glitching');
glitch-test/glitch.js:14:    
glitch-test/glitch.js:15:    let startTime = performance.now();
glitch-test/glitch.js:16:    const duration = 400; // Total transition time
glitch-test/glitch.js:18:    function animate(time) {
glitch-test/glitch.js:19:        let progress = (time - startTime) / duration;
glitch-test/glitch.js:20:        if (progress < 1) {
glitch-test/glitch.js:21:            drawEnderLayers(canvas, img, progress);
glitch-test/glitch.js:22:            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
glitch-test/glitch.js:23:        } else {
glitch-test/glitch.js:24:            canvas.getContext('2d').clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
glitch-test/glitch.js:25:        }
glitch-test/glitch.js:26:    }
glitch-test/glitch.js:27:    requestAnimationFrame(animate);
glitch-test/glitch.js:29:    // Swap source mid-way
glitch-test/glitch.js:30:    currentIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % images.length;
glitch-test/glitch.js:31:    setTimeout(() => { img.src = images[currentIndex]; }, duration / 2);
glitch-test/glitch.js:33:    // End effect
glitch-test/glitch.js:34:    setTimeout(() => { wrapper.classList.remove('glitching'); }, duration);
glitch-test/glitch.js:35:}
glitch-test/glitch.js:37:function drawEnderLayers(canvas, img, progress) {
glitch-test/glitch.js:38:    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
glitch-test/glitch.js:39:    const w = canvas.width;
glitch-test/glitch.js:40:    const h = canvas.height;
glitch-test/glitch.js:42:    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
glitch-test/glitch.js:43:    
glitch-test/glitch.js:44:    // Masking: Draw image first, then only allow painting inside it
glitch-test/glitch.js:45:    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h);
glitch-test/glitch.js:46:    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-atop';
glitch-test/glitch.js:48:    // Defined sensitivity layers [position, thickness, color]
glitch-test/glitch.js:49:    const layers = [
glitch-test/glitch.js:50:        { y: 0.1, th: 0.20, color: 'rgba(100, 32, 167, 0.6)' }, // Void Purple
glitch-test/glitch.js:51:        { y: 0.4, th: 0.10, color: 'rgba(212, 0, 255, 0.8)' }, // End Magenta
glitch-test/glitch.js:52:        { y: 0.7, th: 0.05, color: 'rgba(0, 255, 65, 0.7)' }   // Eye Green
glitch-test/glitch.js:53:    ];
glitch-test/glitch.js:55:    layers.forEach(layer => {
glitch-test/glitch.js:56:        // Move y proportionally
glitch-test/glitch.js:57:        const moveY = ((layer.y + progress) % 1) * h;
glitch-test/glitch.js:58:        const thickness = layer.th * h;
glitch-test/glitch.js:59:        
glitch-test/glitch.js:60:        const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, moveY, 0, moveY + thickness);
glitch-test/glitch.js:61:        grad.addColorStop(0, 'transparent');
glitch-test/glitch.js:62:        grad.addColorStop(0.5, layer.color);
glitch-test/glitch.js:63:        grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
glitch-test/glitch.js:65:        ctx.fillStyle = grad;
glitch-test/glitch.js:66:        // Padding prevents hard edges at the sweep boundaries
glitch-test/glitch.js:67:        ctx.fillRect(0, moveY - (h * 0.1), w, thickness + (h * 0.2));
glitch-test/glitch.js:68:    });

git.bash:181:	reset_credentials () {
git.bash:182:		goto "$REPO_PATH"
git.bash:183:		git config --global --unset credential.helper
git.bash:184:		git config --system --unset credential.helper
git.bash:185:		git config --global user.name "$GH_NAME"
git.bash:186:		git config --global user.email "$GH_EMAIL"
git.bash:187:	}
git.bash:189:	push () {
git.bash:190:		[[ $1 ]] && COMMIT_NAME="$1"
git.bash:191:		echo "PUSHING..."
git.bash:192:		goto "$REPO_PATH"
git.bash:193:		git rm -rf --cached .
git.bash:194:		git add .
git.bash:195:		git commit -m "$COMMIT_NAME"
git.bash:196:		git remote set-url origin "$SSH_REPO_URL"
git.bash:197:		ssh_auth_eval "git push -u origin $BRANCH_NAME"
git.bash:198:	}
git.bash:200:	goto () {
git.bash:201:		cd "$1" || {
git.bash:202:			echo "Info: Cannot CD to $1"
git.bash:203:			exit 1
git.bash:204:		}
git.bash:205:		echo "Info: In $1"
git.bash:206:	}
git.bash:208:	reclone () {
git.bash:209:		local repo_name="$1"
git.bash:210:		rm -rf "$HOME/$repo_name"
git.bash:211:		clone "$repo_name"
git.bash:212:	}
git.bash:213:}
git.bash:215:add_ssh_key_to_ssh_agent () {
git.bash:216:	chmod 600 "$SSH_TRUE_DIR/$SSH_KEY_FILE_NAME"
git.bash:217:	eval "$(ssh-agent -s)"
git.bash:218:	ssh_auth_eval ssh-add "$SSH_TRUE_DIR/$SSH_KEY_FILE_NAME"
git.bash:219:}
git.bash:222:declare_ssh_auth_eval () {
git.bash:223:eval "$(cat <<- "EOF"
git.bash:224:	ssh_auth_eval () {
git.bash:225:		command="$@"
git.bash:226:		ssh_key_passphrase="$SSH_KEY_PASSPHRASE"
git.bash:227:		expect << EOF2
git.bash:228:			spawn $command
git.bash:229:			expect {
git.bash:230:				-re {Enter passphrase for} {
git.bash:231:					send "$ssh_key_passphrase\r"
git.bash:232:					exp_continue
git.bash:233:				}
git.bash:234:				-re {Are you sure you want to continue connecting} {
git.bash:235:					send "yes\r"
git.bash:236:					exp_continue
git.bash:237:				}
git.bash:238:				eof
git.bash:239:			}
git.bash:240:		EOF2
git.bash:241:	}
git.bash:242:EOF
git.bash:243:)"
git.bash:244:}
git.bash:246:main "$@"
